\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_num_c_1_1_methods_a310cc922671bc2da6e1df7ec21c44812}\label{class_num_c_1_1_methods_a310cc922671bc2da6e1df7ec21c44812}} 
\index{Num\+C\+::\+Methods@{Num\+C\+::\+Methods}!arange@{arange}}
\index{arange@{arange}!Num\+C\+::\+Methods@{Num\+C\+::\+Methods}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{arange()}{arange()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename dtype$>$ \\
static \mbox{\hyperlink{class_num_c_1_1_nd_array}{Nd\+Array}}$<$dtype$>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{class_num_c_1_1_methods}{Num\+C\+::\+Methods}}$<$ dtype $>$\+::arange (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{dtype}]{in\+Start,  }\item[{dtype}]{in\+Stop,  }\item[{dtype}]{in\+Step = {\ttfamily 1} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [static]}}

Return evenly spaced values within a given interval.

Values are generated within the half -\/ open interval\mbox{[}start, stop) (in other words, the interval including start but excluding stop). For integer arguments the function is equivalent to the Python built -\/ in range function, but returns an ndarray rather than a list.

When using a non -\/ integer step, such as 0.\+1, the results will often not be consistent.\+It is better to use linspace for these cases.

Num\+Py Reference\+: \href{https://www.numpy.org/devdocs/reference/generated/numpy.arange.html}{\tt https\+://www.\+numpy.\+org/devdocs/reference/generated/numpy.\+arange.\+html}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em start} & value, \\
\hline
{\em stop} & value, \\
\hline
{\em (\+Optional)} & step value, defaults to 1 \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_num_c_1_1_nd_array}{Nd\+Array}} 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Return evenly spaced values within a given interval.

Values are generated within the half -\/ open interval\mbox{[}start, stop) (in other words, the interval including start but excluding stop). For integer arguments the function is equivalent to the Python built -\/ in range function, but returns an ndarray rather than a list.

When using a non -\/ integer step, such as 0.\+1, the results will often not be consistent.\+It is better to use linspace for these cases.

Num\+Py Reference\+: \href{https://www.numpy.org/devdocs/reference/generated/numpy.arange.html}{\tt https\+://www.\+numpy.\+org/devdocs/reference/generated/numpy.\+arange.\+html}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{array\+\_\+equiv()}{array\_equiv()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename dtype$>$ \\
static bool \mbox{\hyperlink{class_num_c_1_1_methods}{Num\+C\+::\+Methods}}$<$ dtype $>$\+::array\+\_\+equiv (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_num_c_1_1_nd_array}{Nd\+Array}}$<$ dtype $>$ \&}]{in\+Array1,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_num_c_1_1_nd_array}{Nd\+Array}}$<$ dtype $>$ \&}]{in\+Array2 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [static]}}

Returns True if input arrays are shape consistent and all elements equal.

\mbox{\hyperlink{class_num_c_1_1_shape}{Shape}} consistent means they are either the same shape, or one input array can be broadcasted to create the same shape as the other one.

Num\+Py Reference\+: \href{https://www.numpy.org/devdocs/reference/generated/numpy.array_equiv.html}{\tt https\+://www.\+numpy.\+org/devdocs/reference/generated/numpy.\+array\+\_\+equiv.\+html}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_num_c_1_1_methods_a193c627a3f91d7de1844414ec5df9b86}\label{class_num_c_1_1_methods_a193c627a3f91d7de1844414ec5df9b86}} 
\index{Num\+C\+::\+Methods@{Num\+C\+::\+Methods}!bincount@{bincount}}
\index{bincount@{bincount}!Num\+C\+::\+Methods@{Num\+C\+::\+Methods}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{bincount()}{bincount()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename dtype$>$ \\
static \mbox{\hyperlink{class_num_c_1_1_nd_array}{Nd\+Array}}$<$dtype$>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{class_num_c_1_1_methods}{Num\+C\+::\+Methods}}$<$ dtype $>$\+::bincount (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_num_c_1_1_nd_array}{Nd\+Array}}$<$ dtype $>$ \&}]{in\+Array,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_num_c_a870ab72deafe3efd4eb63e6a2e63a236}{uint16}}}]{in\+Min\+Length = {\ttfamily 0} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [static]}}

Count number of occurrences of each value in array of non-\/negative ints. Negative values will be counted in the zero bin.

The number of bins(of size 1) is one larger than the largest value in x. If minlength is specified, there will be at least this number of bins in the output array(though it will be longer if necessary, depending on the contents of x).Each bin gives the number of occurrences of its index value in x.

Num\+Py Reference\+: \href{https://www.numpy.org/devdocs/reference/generated/numpy.bincount.html}{\tt https\+://www.\+numpy.\+org/devdocs/reference/generated/numpy.\+bincount.\+html}

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_num_c_1_1_methods_ada3873d1bfea40ccd013b1d7c52a2501}\label{class_num_c_1_1_methods_ada3873d1bfea40ccd013b1d7c52a2501}} 
\index{Num\+C\+::\+Methods@{Num\+C\+::\+Methods}!bincount@{bincount}}
\index{bincount@{bincount}!Num\+C\+::\+Methods@{Num\+C\+::\+Methods}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{bincount()}{bincount()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename dtype$>$ \\
static \mbox{\hyperlink{class_num_c_1_1_nd_array}{Nd\+Array}}$<$dtype$>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{class_num_c_1_1_methods}{Num\+C\+::\+Methods}}$<$ dtype $>$\+::bincount (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_num_c_1_1_nd_array}{Nd\+Array}}$<$ dtype $>$ \&}]{in\+Array,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_num_c_1_1_nd_array}{Nd\+Array}}$<$ dtype $>$ \&}]{in\+Weights,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_num_c_a870ab72deafe3efd4eb63e6a2e63a236}{uint16}}}]{in\+Min\+Length = {\ttfamily 0} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [static]}}

Count number of occurrences of each value in array of non-\/negative ints. Negative values will be counted in the zero bin.

The number of bins(of size 1) is one larger than the largest value in x. If minlength is specified, there will be at least this number of bins in the output array(though it will be longer if necessary, depending on the contents of x).Each bin gives the number of occurrences of its index value in x.\+If weights is specified the input array is weighted by it, i.\+e. if a value n is found at position i, out\mbox{[}n\mbox{]} += weight\mbox{[}i\mbox{]} instead of out\mbox{[}n\mbox{]} += 1. Weights array shall be of the same shape as in\+Array.

Num\+Py Reference\+: \href{https://www.numpy.org/devdocs/reference/generated/numpy.bincount.html}{\tt https\+://www.\+numpy.\+org/devdocs/reference/generated/numpy.\+bincount.\+html}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename dtype$>$ \\
static \mbox{\hyperlink{class_num_c_1_1_nd_array}{Nd\+Array}}$<$bool$>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{class_num_c_1_1_methods}{Num\+C\+::\+Methods}}$<$ dtype $>$\+::isclose (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_num_c_1_1_nd_array}{Nd\+Array}}$<$ dtype $>$ \&}]{in\+Array1,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_num_c_1_1_nd_array}{Nd\+Array}}$<$ dtype $>$ \&}]{in\+Array2,  }\item[{double}]{in\+Rtol = {\ttfamily 1e-\/05},  }\item[{double}]{in\+Atol = {\ttfamily 1e-\/08} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [static]}}

Returns a boolean array where two arrays are element-\/wise equal within a tolerance.

For finite values, isclose uses the following equation to test whether two floating point values are equivalent. absolute(a -\/ b) $<$= (atol + rtol $\ast$ absolute(b))

Num\+Py Reference\+: \href{https://www.numpy.org/devdocs/reference/generated/numpy.isclose.html}{\tt https\+://www.\+numpy.\+org/devdocs/reference/generated/numpy.\+isclose.\+html}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename dtype$>$ \\
static \mbox{\hyperlink{class_num_c_1_1_nd_array}{Nd\+Array}}$<$dtype$>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{class_num_c_1_1_methods}{Num\+C\+::\+Methods}}$<$ dtype $>$\+::linspace (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{dtype}]{in\+Start,  }\item[{dtype}]{in\+Stop,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_num_c_ae685802ca6d3035f2b400b081e3953fa}{uint32}}}]{in\+Num = {\ttfamily 50},  }\item[{bool}]{end\+Point = {\ttfamily true} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [static]}}

Return evenly spaced numbers over a specified interval.

Returns num evenly spaced samples, calculated over the interval\mbox{[}start, stop\mbox{]}.

The endpoint of the interval can optionally be excluded.

Mostly only usefull if called with a floating point type for the template argument.

Num\+Py Reference\+: \href{https://www.numpy.org/devdocs/reference/generated/numpy.linspace.html}{\tt https\+://www.\+numpy.\+org/devdocs/reference/generated/numpy.\+linspace.\+html}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{partition()}{partition()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename dtype$>$ \\
static \mbox{\hyperlink{class_num_c_1_1_nd_array}{Nd\+Array}}$<$dtype$>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{class_num_c_1_1_methods}{Num\+C\+::\+Methods}}$<$ dtype $>$\+::partition (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_num_c_1_1_nd_array}{Nd\+Array}}$<$ dtype $>$ \&}]{in\+Array,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_num_c_ae685802ca6d3035f2b400b081e3953fa}{uint32}}}]{in\+Kth,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_num_c_1_1_axis_a8e689044ef1941a03482e730c5e7ebb3}{Axis\+::\+Type}}}]{in\+Axis = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_num_c_1_1_axis_a8e689044ef1941a03482e730c5e7ebb3a0ae033c4226f7184bf0050b101e7ed94}{Axis\+::\+N\+O\+NE}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [static]}}

Rearranges the elements in the array in such a way that value of the element in kth position is in the position it would be in a sorted array. All elements smaller than the kth element are moved before this element and all equal or greater are moved behind it. The ordering of the elements in the two partitions is undefined.

Num\+Py Reference\+: \href{https://www.numpy.org/devdocs/reference/generated/numpy.partition.html}{\tt https\+://www.\+numpy.\+org/devdocs/reference/generated/numpy.\+partition.\+html}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{putmask()}{putmask()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename dtype$>$ \\
static \mbox{\hyperlink{class_num_c_1_1_nd_array}{Nd\+Array}}$<$dtype$>$\& \mbox{\hyperlink{class_num_c_1_1_methods}{Num\+C\+::\+Methods}}$<$ dtype $>$\+::putmask (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_num_c_1_1_nd_array}{Nd\+Array}}$<$ dtype $>$ \&}]{in\+Array,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_num_c_1_1_nd_array}{Nd\+Array}}$<$ bool $>$ \&}]{in\+Mask,  }\item[{dtype}]{in\+Value }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [static]}}

Changes elements of an array based on conditional and input values.

Sets a.\+flat\mbox{[}n\mbox{]} = values\mbox{[}n\mbox{]} for each n where mask.\+flat\mbox{[}n\mbox{]} == True.

If values is not the same size as a and mask then it will repeat.

Num\+Py Reference\+: \href{https://www.numpy.org/devdocs/reference/generated/numpy.putmask.html}{\tt https\+://www.\+numpy.\+org/devdocs/reference/generated/numpy.\+putmask.\+html}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename dtype$>$ \\

Changes elements of an array based on conditional and input values.

Sets a.\+flat\mbox{[}n\mbox{]} = values\mbox{[}n\mbox{]} for each n where mask.\+flat\mbox{[}n\mbox{]} == True.

If values is not the same size as a and mask then it will repeat.

Num\+Py Reference\+: \href{https://www.numpy.org/devdocs/reference/generated/numpy.putmask.html}{\tt https\+://www.\+numpy.\+org/devdocs/reference/generated/numpy.\+putmask.\+html}
